2016-12-24 00:59:18,198 [7212] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

from sys_roleMenuMap A

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (

  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 11:56:51,736 [7012] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色

  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 12:45:22,996 [8184] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 15:47:26,902 [2652] DEBUG Pyn - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

2016-12-24 17:14:09,083 [6744] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 17:56:46,543 [7844] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 18:50:27,326 [8896] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 19:38:25,201 [7512] DEBUG Sys - 
--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode

2016-12-24 20:22:03,173 [7172] DEBUG Pyn - 
SELECT	sys.columns.name						AS ColumnName, 
		type_name(sys.columns.system_type_id)	AS SqlTypeName,
		sys.columns.max_length					AS MaxLength,
		sys.columns.is_nullable					AS IsNullable,
		sys.columns.is_identity					AS IsIdentity,
		(case when exists(select 1  
						 from   syscolumns 
						 join   sysindexkeys on syscolumns.id  =sysindexkeys.id and syscolumns.colid=sysindexkeys.colid and syscolumns.id=sys.columns.object_id 
						 join   sysindexes   on syscolumns.id  =sysindexes.id   and sysindexkeys.indid=sysindexes.indid   
						 join   sysobjects   on sysindexes.name=sysobjects.name and sysobjects.xtype= 'PK '
						 where syscolumns.name = sys.columns.name) then 1 else 0 end) AS IsPrimaryKey,
		(select value from sys.extended_properties where sys.extended_properties.major_id = sys.columns.object_id and sys.extended_properties.minor_id = sys.columns.column_id) as Description
FROM sys.columns    
WHERE sys.columns.object_id = object_id('undefined')
ORDER BY sys.columns.column_id

from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (

  )  
)

--角色的菜单
select distinct B.*
from sys_roleMenuMap A
inner join sys_menu  B on B.MenuCode = A.MenuCode
where B.IsEnable='1'
  and RoleCode in (
  select RoleCode from sys_userRoleMap where UserCode = 'super' --用户的角色
union all
  select RoleCode from sys_organizeRoleMap where OrganizeCode in  --机构的角色
  (
	select OrganizeCode from sys_userOrganizeMap where UserCode = 'super'
  )  
)
order by B.MenuSeq,B.MenuCode
